***очаг.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:очаг.html>оча́г</a> (4142)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Turkic languages">Turkic</a></span> source;
compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kyrgyz_language" class="extiw" title="w:Kyrgyz language">Kyrgyz</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ky">очок</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ky-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oçok</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,
<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Uzbek_language" class="extiw" title="w:Uzbek language">Uzbek</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="uz">o'choq</i>,
<span class="etylcleanup"><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Turkish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Turkish language">Turkish</a></span></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="tk">ocak</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stove</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>;
from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Turkic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Old Turkic language">Old Turkic</a></span> <i class="Orkh mention" lang="otk">očaq</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="otk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">očaq</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Orkh mention" lang="otk">očuq</i> |  <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="otk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">očuq</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">stove, oven</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очаг.html>оча́г</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">očág</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очаг.html>очага́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очаг.html>очаги́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очаг.html>очаго́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>hearth</li>
<li>pocket <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">an isolated group or area</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:очаг.html>оча́г</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сопротивление.html>сопротивле́ния</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>očág</b> soprotivlénija</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>pocket</b> of resistance</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> breeding ground, hotbed
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:очаг.html>оча́г</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:желтый.html>жёлтой</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лихорадка.html>лихора́дки</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>očág</b> žóltoj lixorádki</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>hotbed</b> of yellow fever</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>(<i>hearth</i>) <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:камин.html>ками́н</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kamín</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li>(<i>hotbed</i>) <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">расса́дник</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">rassádnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очаровать.html>очарова́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">očarovátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ние</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:очевидно.html>очеви́дно</a> (1515)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очевидный.html>очеви́дный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">očevídnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-о</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-o</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очевидно.html>очеви́дно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">očevídno</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>apparently, obviously</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очевидно.html>очеви́дно</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">očevídno</span>)

<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">short neuter singular of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очевидный.html>очеви́дный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">očevídnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***очевидный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:очевидный.html>очеви́дный</a> (3845)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очевидный.html>очеви́дный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">očevídnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>apparent, obvious <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">easily discovered or understood; self-explanatory</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***очень.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a> (87)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown. Often interpreted as inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">*очьнь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">*očĭnĭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> from <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>око</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oko</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">eye</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; the semantic shift might be "visibly gt; obviously gt; prominently gt; very". The non-productive ending is similar to adverbs like <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вкривь.html>вкривь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vkrivʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:впрямь.html>впрямь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vprjamʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">встарь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">vstarʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очень.html>о́чень</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">óčenʹ</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>very, much, very much</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:очередной.html>очередно́й</a> (980)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очередь.html>о́чередь</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óčeredʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">turn, order, rank</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-но́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очередной.html>очередно́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">očerednój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>next (in turn), another</li>
<li>regular</li>
<li>foremost</li>
<li>latest</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очередной.html>очередно́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">očerednój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ость</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ostʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очередность.html>очерёдность</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">očerjódnostʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очередность.html>очерёдности</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>sequence, order of priority
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:установить.html>установи́ть</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:очередность.html>очерёдность</a></b></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ustanovítʹ <b>očerjódnostʹ</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">establish priorities</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:очередность.html>очерёдность</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:претензия.html>прете́нзий</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>očerjódnostʹ</b> pretɛ́nzij/preténzij</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">priority of claims</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:очередность.html>очерёдность</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рассмотрение.html>рассмотре́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:повестка.html>пове́стки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:день.html>дня</a></i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>očerjódnostʹ</b> rassmotrénija povéstki dnja</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">order of the agenda; order of business</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очерченный.html>оче́рченный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">očérčennyj</span>)

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очистить.html>очи́стить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">očístitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<ol><li>to clear oneself</li>
<li>to clear</li>
<li>to become purer

***очистка.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:очистка.html>очи́стка</a> (9668)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очистить.html>очи́стить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">očístitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очистка.html>очи́стка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">očístka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очистка.html>очи́стки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очистка.html>очи́стки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очистка.html>очи́сток</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">очистно́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>cleaning, purification, clearing, refinement</li>
<li>peeling</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">military</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mopping-up</li>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очищаться.html>очища́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">očiščátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очиститься.html>очи́ститься</a></b>)

<ol><li>to clear oneself</li>
<li>to clear</li>
<li>to become purer

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:очищать.html>очища́ющий</a> (9977)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***очко.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очко</a> (1106)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>о́ко</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óko</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">eye</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ко́</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-kó</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; originally a diminutive..
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очко́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">očkó</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очка́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очки́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очко́в</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>point</li>
<li>spot, pip <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">on cards or dice</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li>hole, peephole</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> eye</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> asshole, anus</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ability to stay calm and adequate while under pressure in a stressful situation</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> toilet (bowl)
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2018</b>,  <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/ru:%D0%9A%D1%80%D0%BE%D0%B2%D0%BE%D1%81%D1%82%D0%BE%D0%BA" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:ru:Кровосток">Кровосток</a></span> (lyrics and music),  “<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:злой.html>злы́е</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:голубь.html>го́луби</a></span>”, in  <cite><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">ЧБ</span></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:устроить.html>устро́ил</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>смерть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очко́м</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сортир.html>сорти́ре</a><br /><a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>Смерть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очко́м</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>смерть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:над.html>над</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>очко́м</a></b></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ustróil smertʹ nad <b>očkóm</b> v sortíre<br />Smertʹ nad <b>očkóm</b>, smertʹ nad <b>očkóm</b></i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I’ve caused a death on a toilet in the loo<br />Death on the bowl, death on the bowl</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">card games</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> blackjack</li></ol>

***очнуться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:очнуться.html>очну́ться</a> (2981)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">ѡчхнꙋтисѧ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">očxnutisę</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*otjьtnǫti sę</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очнуться.html>очну́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">očnútʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to awaken</li>
<li>to come to, to gain consciousness</li>
<li>to come to one's senses</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:очный.html>о́чный</a> (17323)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очко.html>о́ко</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">óko</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

</p>
<ol><li>face to face</li>

<dl><dd><span class="nyms antonym"><span class="defdate">Antonym:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заочный.html>зао́чный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">zaóčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">distance education</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:очутившийся.html>очути́вшийся</a> (3716)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очутившийся.html>очути́вшийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">očutívšijsja</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active perfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очутиться.html>очути́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">očutítʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***очутиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:очутиться.html>очути́ться</a> (3716)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">очꙋтитисꙗ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">očutitisja</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to find oneself, to come to be</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">очꙋтити</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">očutiti</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to notice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*oťutiti</i>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ощутить.html>ощути́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">oščutítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a borrowing from Old Church Slavonic. 
</p><p>Unrelated to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чуять.html>чу́ять</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čújatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чувство.html>чу́вство</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čúvstvo</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, etc.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очутиться.html>очути́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">očutítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to find oneself (suddenly) in a place</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be found (in a place)</li></ol>

***очухаться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:очухаться.html>очу́хаться</a> (11901)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From a root related to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очнуться.html>очну́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">očnútʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-atʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:очухаться.html>очу́хаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">očúxatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vernacular</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to come to oneself, to come to one's senses</li></ol>
